Tags: ['STOPRUSSIA', 'АГРЕСІЯ РФ', 'ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ']

Category: News

Photo illustrative

Fleeing the war, much of the Ukrainians found shelter in the countries of the europe. According to the King Institute of the World Economy, governor of European countries have spent more than 43 billionurov on Ukrainians.

About it reportsMinistry of Inquiring Reintegration of Temporarily Occupied Territories.

"Such expenses include cash payments, housing, medical care, educational services, as well as providing food and first -time foods," the statement reads.

Poland has spent more than 12 billion euros among European countries that accept Ukrainians. In the second place, Germany was in this indicator. It costs for Ukrainian asylum seekers almost 11 billion euros.

Significant funds for shelter for Ukrainians were spent by the Czech Republic(2.94 billion euros),Spain(2.24 billion euros), France(2.04 billion euros), Romania(EUR 1.26 billion),Switzerland(EUR 1.16 billion)and Italy(EUR 1.15 billion).

Category: News

A year ago, the Center for Studies of Military History of Armed Forces was formed. During this period of time, the military scientific institution has acquired the ability to fully fulfill the tasks identified by the management of the Armed Forces of Ukraine.

In particular, during the year of existence of the Center, 8 essays on the history of the Russian-Ukrainian war, 8 scientific articles were published, 2 monographs and 1 collection of documents were developed. 7 scientific conferences, seminars and round tables were organized and held. Developed and sent to the bodies of military management, scientific institutions and universities of 11 issues of monthly "military-historicalhops of the Russian-Ukrainian war".

!(Images/AРМІЯINFORM/2023-07-05T98-00-00-04-00/img_0351-150x150.jpg)

In addition, 6 exhibition projects were implemented. This is in particular exhibitions "The Signature of the Holy Intercession", "The Modern Army through the Prism of the Past", "February: The Field of Non -Turnover", "The Union of White Eagle and the Golden Trizub" and more. Not only did the whole exhibition projects be presented to the wide collaboration in the capital of Ukraine, but also exhibited in regional and district centers, as well as in many educational and educational institutions, military parts. For example, the exhibition project "Modern Army through the Prism", the main purpose of which is to restore the historical memory of the university on the development and imitation of military traditions of the Ukrainian millilic formations of the first half of the twentieth century, which continue to live in the modern armory forces Generations in the protection of their statehood, exhibited in the west of Ukraine, also attack in the central regions.

According to the Deputy Chief of the General Staff of the Armed Forces of Ukraine, the General-Major Volodymyr Koval, the Center for Studies of Military History of Armed Forces of Ukraine makes it a daily contribution to our victory. Its staff is forming Ukraine and spreading the historical truth.

!(Images/AРМІЯINFORM/2023-07-05T98-00-00-04-00/img_0617-2-150x150.jpg)

-The staff of the Center successfully combines theory with practice, became a focus, defect the main and significant historical events for the armed forces and the state, very important for the further formation of Ukraine as the modern European state and celebrating the role of the Ukrainian army in this historical process,-said Major General Vladimir. During the festivities.

Deputy Chief of the General Staff of Ukraine Major General Volodymyr Koval

On the occasion of the anniversary of the Center for the best scientists and workers, the awards of the Minister of Defense and the Commander -in -Chief of the Armed Forces of Ukraine were awarded. Military historians also demonstrated the exhibition "Modern Army through the Prism of the Past", which will soon be presented in military educational establishments and institutions of the Armory Forces of Ukraine.

Violation of Operation of block # 5 of the ZPP can cause a large -scale release of radiation - Energoatom

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-07-06T-9:20:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-07-06T21:20:00+03:00

Description: Violation of the basic requirements for operation of the unit No. 5 of Zaporizhzhya NPP, in particular, the refusal of the Russians to bring it to the state of the cold stop, can lead to an accident. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16621...']

Tags: ['Аварія', 'Енергоатом', 'Радіація', 'Запорізька АЕС']

Type: Article

Violation of basic requirements for operation of the unit No. 5 of Zaporizhzhya NPP, in particular, the refusal of the Russians to bring it to the state of "Cold stop", can lead to an accident.

About it reports NAEK "Energoatom" in telegram, reports Ukrinform

The company reminds that the unit # 5 of the Zaporizhzhya NPP was introduced by vexplaination more than 34 years ago. And in order to maintain safe operation, the block must be provided with timely and quality maintenance of taremont equipment, without which operation becomes dangerous.

Instead, since the beginning of a full -scale invasion, the Block has worked at power levels, and since September 2022 the occupation of the station has supported his work in a hot stop.

Energoatom states that the invaders deliberately violate the number of basic requirements for the operation of the power unit, including ignoring the planned schedule of maintenance of safety systems, sabotage of overhaul of the reactor ward and current repair of thermal mechanical, electrical equipment of the turbine.

Read also: IAEA asks for additional access to reactors ZPP –GrossiIn addition, the service life of the equipment that is subject to replacement is exhausted. In particular, it is more than 1000 units of thermal mechanical equipment more 100 - electrical.

“The complex of these violations has serious consequences and many times increases the risk of systems that can lead to an emergency. In this case, the countries of Europe may be affected by radiation influence, ”the company warns.

SE "NNEGC" Energoatom ", in order to implement the decision of the State Inspectorate of Nuclear Regulation of Ukraine, repeatedly called for the transfer of power unit # 5 of the ZNPU more secure regime -" Cold stop ". Last week Diara sent a letter to IAEAcalling for an order. Despite the involvement in the process of international organizations, all efforts do not reach.

In response to the requests of the Armed Forces of Ukraine and the Ministry of Internal Affairs of Ukraine, with the support of NATO programs from the transition from a military career to a civilian, within the framework of the complex help of assistance to Ukraine(Efficiency), the implementation of the project of zapsychological rehabilitation and the restoration of psychological stability of troops of servicemen began. About it reportsThe General Staff of the Armed Forces.

!(Images/AРМІЯINFORM/2023-07-06T0-00-00-04-00/358074551_617566707223078_6754904855657052342_n-150x150.jpg)

It is noted that the practical implementation of the project is provided by the NGO "League of Officers", which since 2014 has been working systematically in the direction of psychological support of military servicemen.

In 2023, 65 three -day trainings for the personnel involved in the tasks in the fighting areas were planned. Training for the work of practical psychological skills, backed by theoretical knowledge.

Soldiers master the methods of providing the first psychological self -help of assistance to brothers in combat according to recognized international practices and protocols. During the trainings, measures for overcoming non-negative mental states, learning the techniques of emotional and volitional mobilization and individual psychological counseling of the military personnel who interfere with this.

This project is a continuation of NATO representation activities in Ukraine in spherushological rehabilitation for the subjects of the security and defense sector, successfully reserved during 2014-2019.

The new project is the answer to the urgent need for training and psychological training of the personnel of the Defense Forces of Ukraine and is aimed at acquiring their life -long psychological assistance skills in the conditions of hostilities.

Zelensky signed a new version of the Consumer Protection Act

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-07-06T15:52:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-07-06T15:52:00+03:00

Description: On July 5, President of Ukraine Volodymyr Zelensky signed a new version of the Law on Consumer Protection. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16878...']

Tags: ['Закон', 'Харчування', 'Споживчий кошик', 'Зеленський']

Type: Article

On July 5, Presidential of Ukraine signed a new version of the Law on Consumer Protection on July 5.

According to Ukrinform, it reports the State Service of Ukraine on Food and Consumer Protection.It is noted that the law was developed in order to bring national consumer protection to the legislation of the European Union for harmonization of consumer protection system in Ukraine with the principles, approaches and practices of the EU.

In particular, the document actualizes the definitions and terms and leads them to the conditions of modern business, including on e -commerce(Internet trade).

Читайте також: Україна зможе експортувати овець та кіз до ЛівануThe updated version of the law envisages the creation of a single state consumer web -portal in the field of e -commerce(E-buyer portal). Ця електроннасистема буде збирати, накопичувати, обробляти, вести облік та надаватиспоживачам інформацію про суб’єктів електронної комерції, їхні комунікації,споживачів, а також про органи державної влади, які здійснюють захист правспоживачів у відповідних сферах.

Закон також передбачає створення автоматизованої системи перевірених продавців– інформаційної системи, яка стане складовою частиною порталу е-покупець.

Крім цього, документ визначає права споживача у разі придбання непридатного чинебезпечного харчового продукту.

Закон дозволяє вводити обмеження доступу до вебсайту суб’єкта господарюванняза зверненням Держпродспоживслужби до провайдера у разі порушеннязаконодавства таким суб’єктом господарювання.

Читайте також: В Україні продовжили регулювання цін на деякі продукти уперіод воєнного стану The law also provides for new powers of the State Consumer Service: interaction of economic entities, consumers and other CEBs on the portal of the e-buyer; filing lawsuits for the protection of consumer rights, including the unreserved range of consumers; to take measures provided for by law, the economic entities - manufacturers of goods.The law stipulates that information on products cannot be provided by the language of the aggressor or occupier state. Thus, they emphasized in the department, strengthened the requirements set out in the current laws of Ukraine "On Consumer Protection" and "On Ensuring the Functioning of the Ukrainian Language as a State Language".

Read also: in Kiev daily record up to 30 violations for trade products food Law(except for some provisions)It will enter into force one year from the date of its publication, but not earlier than the day of termination or abolition of martial law.

According to Ukrinform, the Verkhovna Rada adopted a new version of the Law of Consumer Protection in the second reading on June 10, 2023.

June 2023 was recognized as warmest in history

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-07-06T16:00:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-07-06T16:00:00+03:00

Description: June 2023 became the hottest June in the history of observations in the world. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16886...']

Tags: ['Клімат', 'Рекорд', 'Спека']

Type: Article

June2023 became the hottest June in the history of observations in the world.

As Ukrinform reports, this is stated in press releaseEU climate change services Copernicus.

“The moon was the warmestJune all over the world with a temperature slightly more than 0.5 ° C above the average indicator for 1991-2020. The previous record of June 2019 was significantly up, ”the service said.

It is noted that record temperatures of June 2023 were observed in a semi -nervous event of Europe.

In addition, parts of Canada, the United States, Mexico, Asia and Eastern Australia were much warmer than usual.

At the same time, in the West of Australia and the United States and in the western part of Russia, it was cooler than usual.

Also, the surface temperature of the sea in the oceans was higher than in any pre-June.

Read also: in the world recorded the hottest day in the history of consultationsAmong other things, the EU climates indicate that Antarctic Sea Ice has reached the lowest level since the beginning of satellite observations. His indicator was 17% below the average, which also became a new record.

As reported by Ukrinform, according to the report of the International Center for Integrated Mountains(Icimod), glaciers in the Himalayas can lose up to 75% of their volume by the end of 2100 due to global warming.

Read also: Duda hopes for weakening from September 15th restrictions on the import of Ukrainian Consecration Zhaya to the EUAccording to him, all EU -neighboring country with Ukraine urge the European Commission to have a ban on importing Ukrainian grain by the end of the year.

*!(https://www.ukrinform.ua/rubric-economy/3726892-import-ukrainskogo-zbizza-u-polsi-proveli-perevirku-v-222-kompaniah.html)He noted that in the near future he will also speak on this topic with the Minister of Supreme Economy of Lithuania, which did not join the countries that require an embargoo for Ukrainian grain.

In May 2023, the European Commission forbade the import of wheat, corn, rapeseed and sunflower from Ukraine to Bulgaria, Hungary, Poland, Slovakia and Romania at the insistence of these countries. On June 5, the prohibition was proceeded by September 15, 2023.Poland has suspended transit of Ukrainian agro -agricultural products through its territory, but renewed it from April 21.

Warsaw hopes that the ban on import of Ukrainian grain will be reinforced and after September 15, and that some other types of products from Ukraine will be added to the list of prohibited products.

One of the arguments of Warsaw to ban the import of Ukrainian grain to Poland, the import of technical grain, which was later sold as a consumer, as well as the passage of a large amount of Ukrainian grain to the Polish market, from which Polish agrarians were present.

The parliamentary elections in Poland will probably take place in October. The exact Datuvibor President of Poland should be indicated by mid -August.

Bulgaria Parliament supported Ukraine's membership in NATO

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Publisher: Укринформ (Organization)

Published Time: 2023-07-06T16:45:00+03:00

Modified Time: 2023-07-06T16:45:00+03:00

Description: Bulgaria's Parliament approved a declaration to support Ukraine's membership in NATO. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16878...']

Tags: ['Болгарія', 'НАТО', 'Україна', 'Стефанчук']

Type: Article

Parliamentbulgaria adopted a declaration to support Ukraine's membership in NATO.

This was reported by the Verkhovna Rada Chairman Ruslan Stefanchuk in Facebook, reports Ukrinform.

“The Bulgaria Parliament has approved a declaration in support of Ukraine's membership in NATO. I am grateful for this decision!” - the speaker wrote.

According to him, the document states that the Bulgarian People's Assembly expects that the government, in particular at the future of the Alliance Summit in Vilnius, will express the position of support for Ukraine's membership in NATOAfter peace is restored in its territory.

In addition, Stefanchuk said, the Bulgaria Parliament supports the Procedure of Planning and Adoption of Specific Parameters and Time Frames of NATO Entrance, deepening political and practical support by the Alliance and expanding strategic relations.

Bulgaria's parliamentarians also urge the Allies to use Vilnius Samite to outline clear parameters on the path to Ukraine's membership in NATO, the Verkhovna Rada added.

Read also: Bulgaria Prime Minister awaits a new meeting with Zelensky NATO NATO in VilniusAs reports The Sofia Globe, Bulgaria's People's Assembly voted a significant majority of the declaration of the Declaration, which contains a call to the government at the July NATO Summit to express support for Ukraine's accession to NATO after the NATO peace resumes.

Of the 214 deputies who voted, 157 - were "for". Among them are the deputies of the parties of the Gerb-SDS, "We continue changes", "Movement for rights and freedoms"(MRF)But "there is such a people." There were 57 votes on the Renaissance and the Bulgarian Passonic Party.

The Declaration expresses full support for the NATO open door policy, independent of external factors, and there is a call to the members of the Alliance outlined parameters on the way to Ukraine's membership in NATO.The national meeting of the country categorically demand to immediately stop the nuclear -shade, as well as all actions of the Russian Federation, which sharply contradict the UN Charter, which is the most serious blow to peace and prosperity of both the European and Irosian people.

The formula of peace of President of Ukraine Volodymyr Zelensky is also supported, the purpose of which is a strong and just peace.

This can be achieved through the use of state funds as a "catalyst" to inflow private investment, in particular to maintain risky and "breakthrough" innovative projects. Type: Article

Finland has disseminated restrictions on entry and transit in its territory of Russian citizens.

As Ukrinform reports, this is reported on siteFinland Foreign Ministry.

As it is noted, the previously introduced ban on tourist travel of citizens of the Russian Federation will be preserved, as well as transit travel for them through FinlandOther Schengen countries. Restrictions for business travelers, homeowners and students will be strengthened.

From now on, Russian citizens who go on a business trip will only be banned from Finnish border. In addition, it will be necessary to prove that such a businessman really has a valid reason for arrival.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Modified Time: 2023-07-06T20:11:00+03:00

Description: The United States called on the UN Secretariat for 30 days to inform the Radbez about the use of Iranian drones in the war against Ukraine. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16661...']

Tags: ['Безпілотник', 'Іран', 'ООН', 'Росія', 'Дрон', 'Радбез ООН']

Type: Article

The United States of America called on the UN Secretariat for 30 days to inform the Soviet Union for the use of Iranian drones in the war against Ukraine.

According to Ukrinform correspondent in New York, a UN Radsebz Council was stated on Thursday at the United States by UN Landa Thomas Grinfield.

She indicated that Russia was using Iranian drones against Ukrainian largest and civilian infrastructure. Over the past few weeks, the Russian Federation has repeatedly implemented attacks with the help of these UAVs, which has led to the destruction of Ukrainian civilian objects and the death of civilians.

"Moreover, we have shared publicly with the secretariat that the Russian was working with Iran on the production of Iranian UAVs in Russia," emphasize Grinfield. - In particular, Russia receives from Iran the materials needed for the construction of the production plant UAVin Russia".

According to her, this plant can be commissioned in the early year. In the event of construction, it "will significantly strengthen the potential for the attack on Ukraine and will allow Russia to continue the campaign of disruption of Ukrainian power plants, the closure of railways and to interfere with the transit of agricultural goods into world markets," the post -press.

Read also: Supply of weapons from Iran to Russia has become regular ignat"The UN Secretariat is obliged to fulfill its mandate to study the proof of Iran's programs for unmanned aerial vehicles of Russia in violation of paragraph 4 of the appendix in the UN Resolution 2231," she stressed.

Thomas Grinfield has regretted the fact that the reported non-proliferation of nuclear weapons is published today, "is incomplete because it does not fully covers the recent violations associated with unmanned aircraft."

According to her, the Secretariat did not accept proposals from Ukraine and other sides to consider the undeniable evidence of these violations. "This is a unclear gap," she added.

"The UN should, without any further delay, send a group of investigators to study the wreckage of weapons that Russia uses against Ukraine and which is blocked by Ukraine and the United Kingdom," Thomas Grinfield emphasized.Iranian development and dissemination of UAV is a global threat, explained. This has consequences not only for peace and security in the Middle East, but also for Ukraine and the rest of the world.

“I again urge the UN Secretariat to inform the Council about its assessment of the Iranian blessings found in Ukraine for the next 30 days. It is a question of life or death for the Ukrainian people and the nation of Ukraine as an economically viable state, ”she stressed.

As reported by Ukrinform, the Ukrainian delegation took part in the UN Radion Security meetingRegarding the Iranian nuclear program.

The UN Security Council resolution 2231 was approved on July 20, 2015 within the framework of a comprehensive action plan for Iran's nuclear program.

The document contains provisions that restrict Iran in obtaining and transmitting technologies, including drones, for eight years of depositing the agreement - by the second half of 2023(paragraph 4 of the Annex).

What is threads? It is an analogue of Twitter that launched Meta.

Modified Time: 2023-07-06T21:20:00+03:00

Description: Violation of the basic requirements for operation of the unit No. 5 of Zaporizhzhya NPP, in particular, the refusal of the Russians to bring it to the state of the cold stop, can lead to an accident. - Ukrinform.

Images: ['630_360_16621...']

Tags: ['Аварія', 'Енергоатом', 'Радіація', 'Запорізька АЕС']

Type: Article

Violation of basic requirements for operation of the unit No. 5 of Zaporizhzhya NPP, in particular, the refusal of the Russians to bring it to the state of "Cold stop", can lead to an accident.

About it reports NAEK "Energoatom" in telegram, reports Ukrinform

The company reminds that the unit # 5 of the Zaporizhzhya NPP was introduced by vexplaination more than 34 years ago. And in order to maintain safe operation, the block must be provided with timely and quality maintenance of taremont equipment, without which operation becomes dangerous.

Instead, since the beginning of a full -scale invasion, the Block has worked at power levels, and since September 2022 the occupation of the station has supported his work in a hot stop.

Energoatom states that the invaders deliberately violate the number of basic requirements for the operation of the power unit, including ignoring the planned schedule of maintenance of safety systems, sabotage of overhaul of the reactor ward and current repair of thermal mechanical, electrical equipment of the turbine.

Read also: IAEA asks for additional access to reactors ZPP –GrossiIn addition, the service life of the equipment that is subject to replacement is exhausted. In particular, it is more than 1000 units of thermal mechanical equipment more 100 - electrical.

“The complex of these violations has serious consequences and many times increases the risk of systems that can lead to an emergency. In this case, the countries of Europe may be affected by radiation influence, ”the company warns.

SE "NNEGC" Energoatom ", in order to implement the decision of the State Inspectorate of Nuclear Regulation of Ukraine, repeatedly called for the transfer of power unit # 5 of the ZNPU more secure regime -" Cold stop ". Last week Diara sent a letter to IAEAcalling for an order. Despite the involvement in the process of international organizations, all efforts do not reach.

Government's decision brought the donor blood closer to the front

Author: ['АРМІЯINFORM']

Time: 2023-07-06T91:00:00-04:00

Description: Podn 60% of deaths for half the battle of the ili iz. As soon as he is overflowing the bloody blood ... War with Ukraine 2022, the war with Ukraine is the latest news today, the news war with Ukraine 2022 The last for today, will there be a war between Ukraine and Russia, and when, the war with Ukraine in 2022 will be or not, will there be whether it will be, will it be The war with Ukraine in the near future says, the war with Ukraine, Ukrainian news today, Ukrainian news in Ukrainian media in Russian

Images: ['donory.jpeg']

Tags: ['STOPRUSSIA', 'АГРЕСІЯ РФ', 'ВІЙНА', 'ВТОРГНЕННЯ РФ', 'ДОНОРИ КРОВІ', 'КАБІНЕТ МІНІСТРІВ УКРАЇНИ', 'МОЗ УКРАЇНИ']

Category: News

More than 60% of battle deaths are related to blood loss. Timely transfusion of healing blood or its components can significantly reduce this percentage, as it will allow you to win time to send the wounded to the nearest hospital.

This is on a single webport of the executive authorities of Ukraine notesMinistry of Health.

Every day, defenders and defenders of Ukraine heroically defend the peace of Ukraine. Each of them risks their own life and health for peace, victory and restoration of our territorial integrity.

In war, there are injuries and injuries that are incompatible with life. However, there are also tissues that can be prevented. It is about heroes with massive blood loss. In a timely wounds timely stopping of bleeding - only the first stage of assistance. The second stage is no less important. It involves the recovery of the blood that has been saved. Timely transfusion(transfusion)The whole donor blood can save more than one life by the supra.

The resolution developed by the Ministry of Health must streamline the mechanism of donor blood and its components and bring them closer to the front. Counterly identifies and regulates the logistics chains of obtaining a donor civil and its components with medical units. Without unnecessary bureaucracy of the paneoptimally organized procedures.

From now on, the mechanism of security and defense forces in donor blood deals with the request for the required blood volumes from combat units. According to the opportunity to prepare and deliver to the war zone in time.

The resolution also stipulates that each medical unit determines the person responsible for the order of donor blood and its components. At the same time, doctors independently decide how they are more convenient to order blood - branches or from individual medical units. This makes the system flexible to the operational situation on the front.

The process of obtaining donor blood and its components with medical units of force safety and defense is simple and understandable. It provides such an algorithm of action:In fact, the tasks of the units are reduced to the formation of applications and reports in which the responsible persons of medical units provide a minimum necessary information. This approach allows military doctors to spend optimally one time and do not make unnecessary efforts to find and ensure the delivery of a donor blood and its components.

At the same time, the resolution defined the algorithm of actions of medical units in critical situations, such as the mass receipt of the wounded. In this case, medical units can take away the required amount of Donor Claw and its components in the auxiliary temporary blood bank, which will only be known to them as quickly as possible.

In addition, medical units will now be able to send their nursing staff to the blood centers for training of transfusions. As the result - the implementation of this resolution will facilitate the provision of medical services to medical services in accordance with NATO standards set by TCSS protocols(Tactical Сombat Сasualty Сare).

"I said frankly: if Russia goes on, your weapon will not be enough. Even if it will be five times more than you have now. Our weapons were also not enough - we were helped by partners, ”Volodymyr Zelenskyy emphasized.“And if some leaders are very pragmatic, at least from this point of view to understand: while Ukrainians are fighting - help them. Otherwise, there is a probability that every one will come to you, ”the head of state said.

The President also noted that for the Ukrainian people a very important motivational factor would be a clear signal of the prospect of acquiring Ukraine's membership in NATO at a summit in Vilnius, as it was with the granting of EU members in June 2022.

“We understand that in NATO we will be in a few years or after the war - how the members of the Alliance will be. But it is necessary to give a signal to motivate Ukraine to protect Europe. This is not such a high price for such a war and for such suffering, ”Volodymyr Zelenskyy recalled.

Authors: Ukrinform (Person)

Type: Article

Negotiation of the final documents of the NATO summit in Vilnius for Ukraine is still ongoing, and there are no final agreed decisions at this time.

This was stated by Viceremier-Minister for European and Euro-Atlantic Integration Olga Stephanyshyn on the broadcasting of the only news, the Ukrinform correspondent reports.

“From a practical point of view, there are enough experiences and decisions will already be announced during the summit. Moreover, there is a discussion on security guarantees, which, including NATO's individual Universities - today the Alliance has no objection to this format, ”she said.

Read also: Zelensky called NATO in Vilnius to motivate Ukraine: this is not such a high price for sufferingAt the same time, the Viceremier emphasized that the guarantees did not replace Valiance's membership.

“We have demonstrated our ability as a state in a full -scale conditions and, accordingly, insist that we are ready to prepare Ukraine from NATO's support for Ukraine, but we need specific decisions and political decisions. Political invitation to membership is possible at the summit of the reconciliation, the final arrangements are not yet, talking with the leaders is ongoing, ”Stephanyshyn said.

She did not rule out that the final discussions would be held in the summit fields.

Read also: Bulgaria's viceremier called the EU and NATO Consecration of UkraineIt was reported that on July 11-12, a NATO summit will take place in Vilnius, during which Ukraine wants to receive clear security guarantees and a clear perspective of the Alliance.
